A Contract For Difference (CFD) is a contract between a buyer and a seller. They agree that the seller pays the difference between the opening price and the closing price. CFD is an investment instrument with a leverage function with which you, the investor, can make money with both rising and falling rates. Thanks to leverage, you can buy currency pairs for a multiple of the amount that you invest with CFD. \r\n\r\nThe Forex app consists of the following chapters:\r\n1.\tWhat is Forex?\r\n2.\tAn explanation of Forex rates\r\n3.\tHow do I fulfil a Forex position?\r\n4.\tAn Forex strategy for beginners\r\n5.\tRisk management\r\n6.\tPractical examples\r\n7.\tBrokers: getting started with Forex trade\r\n\r\nAfter you complete the Forex course you know what Forex is and how the currency market works.
